Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1275, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 305. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

Classified issues

Issue contentBeyondLandmarks

WCAG: 1.3.6

Score: 182

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r57, score 146 (Perceivable text content is not included in any landmark)
  • Package axe, test region, score 24 (Some page content is not contained by landmarks)
  • Package ibm, test Rpt_Aria_OrphanedContent_Native_Host_Sematics, score 62 (Content does not reside within an element with a landmark role)

Issue duplicateID

WCAG: 4.1.1

Score: 126

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package ibm, test RPT_Elem_UniqueId, score 124 (Element id attribute value is not unique within the document)

Issue linkForcesNewWindow

WCAG: 3.2.5

Score: 65

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 218, score 63 (Link opens in a new window without user control)

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 44

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 4 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package qualWeb, test QW-ACT-R62, score 40 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue textContrastAA

WCAG: 1.4.3

Score: 42

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package alfa, test r69, score 5 (Text outside widget has subminimum contrast)
  • Package axe, test color-contrast, score 35 (Element has insufficient color contrast)
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G18.Fail, score 4 (Contrast between the text and its background is less than 4.5:1)
  • Package wave, test c:contrast, score 3 (Very low contrast)

Issue linkIndication

WCAG: 1.3.3

Score: 36

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test linkUl, score 34 (Non-underlined adjacent links)

Issue fontSizeAbsolute

Score: 28
